-- This will create the SQL_CLASS and SQL_VIEWS databases on Snowflake.
-- Select access need to be granted on views and tables on these schemas.
-- At the end of this script is sql which will remove these databases from your system.
-- You may need to modify the script to fit your systems particular requirements
-- but do not change any object names or the join builder demo will not work.
-- If you have any installation issues, please contact helpdesk@coffingdw.com.

CREATE DATABASE NEXUS;
USE DATABASE NEXUS;
CREATE SCHEMA SQL_CLASS;
CREATE SCHEMA SQL_VIEWS;

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.CUSTOMER_TABLE
 (CUSTOMER_NUMBER  INTEGER, CUSTOMER_NAME VARCHAR(20), PHONE_NUMBER CHAR(8));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.ORDER_TABLE
 (ORDER_NUMBER INTEGER, CUSTOMER_NUMBER INTEGER, ORDER_DATE  DATE, ORDER_TOTAL DECIMAL(10,2) );
 
CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.STUDENT_TABLE
 (STUDENT_ID INTEGER, LAST_NAME CHAR(20), FIRST_NAME VARCHAR(12), CLASS_CODE  CHAR(2) , GRADE_PT  DECIMAL(5,2) );

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.COURSE_TABLE
 (COURSE_ID SMALLINT, COURSE_NAME  VARCHAR(30), CREDITS INTEGER, SEATS  INTEGER);

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.STUDENT_COURSE_TABLE
 (STUDENT_ID INTEGER, COURSE_ID   SMALLINT);
 
CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.SALES_TABLE
 (PRODUCT_ID INTEGER, SALE_DATE  DATE, DAILY_SALES  DECIMAL(9,2));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.EMPLOYEE_TABLE
 (EMPLOYEE_NO INTEGER, DEPT_NO SMALLINT, LAST_NAME CHAR(20), FIRST_NAME VARCHAR(12), SALARY  DECIMAL(8,2) );

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.DEPARTMENT_TABLE
 (DEPT_NO SMALLINT, DEPARTMENT_NAME CHAR(20), 
 MGR_NO  INTEGER, BUDGET  DECIMAL(10,2));
 
CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.STATS_TABLE
 (COL1 SMALLINT, COL2 SMALLINT, COL3 SMALLINT, COL4 SMALLINT, 
 COL5 SMALLINT, COL6 SMALLINT);

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.JOB_TABLE 
 (JOB_NO INT NOT NULL UNIQUE, JOB_DESC VARCHAR(20));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.EMP_JOB_TABLE
 (JOB_NO INT, EMP_NO INT);

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.NAMES_TABLE
 (NAME VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL UNIQUE);

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.HIERARCHY_TABLE 
(EMPLOYEE_NO INTEGER 
,DEPT_NO SMALLINT
,FIRST_NAME VARCHAR(12)
,LAST_NAME CHAR(20) 
,SALARY DECIMAL (10,2) 
,POSITION_NAME CHAR (20) 
,MGR_EMPLOYEE_NO INTEGER 
);

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.ADDRESSES
 (SUBSCRIBER_NO INTEGER, STREET VARCHAR(30), CITY VARCHAR(20), STATE CHAR(2), ZIP INTEGER, AREACODE SMALLINT, PHONE INTEGER);

CREATE  TABLE SQL_CLASS.SUBSCRIBERS
 (SUBSCRIBER_NO INTEGER, MEMBER_NO SMALLINT, LAST_NAME CHAR(20), FIRST_NAME VARCHAR(20), GENDER CHAR(1), SSN INTEGER);
  
CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.CLAIMS
 (CLAIM_ID INTEGER, CLAIM_DATE DATE, CLAIM_SERVICE SMALLINT, SUBSCRIBER_NO INTEGER, MEMBER_NO SMALLINT, CLAIM_AMT DECIMAL(12,2), PROVIDER_NO SMALLINT);

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.PROVIDERS
 (PROVIDER_CODE  SMALLINT, PROVIDER_NAME   VARCHAR(30), P_ADDRESS VARCHAR(30), P_CITY  VARCHAR(20), P_STATE CHAR(2), P_ZIP  INT, P_ERROR_RATE  DEC(4,4));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.SERVICES
 (SERVICE_CODE  SMALLINT, SERVICE_DESC  VARCHAR(30), SERVICE_PAY  DECIMAL(7,2));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.BANK_SALES 
 (PRODUCT_ID NUMBER(38,0),  PRODUCT_NAME VARCHAR(20), SALE_DATE TIMESTAMP_NTZ(6), DAILY_SALES NUMBER(15,2));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.EMPLOYEE_PHONE 
 (FIRST_NAME VARCHAR(20),  LAST_NAME VARCHAR(20),  DEPT_NO NUMBER(38,0),  HOME_PHONE VARCHAR(20), WORK_PHONE VARCHAR(20),  CELL_PHONE VARCHAR(20));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.LAT_LONG 
  (STATE VARCHAR(32),   LATITUDE NUMBER(11,0),   LONGITUDE NUMBER(11,0));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.PIVOT_TEST_REGION_ALL 
  (REGION VARCHAR(20),   SALES_PERSON VARCHAR(30),   PRODUCT VARCHAR(20),   QUANTITY NUMBER(11,0),   COST NUMBER(10,2),   SALE_DATE DATE,   DAILY_SALES NUMBER(10,2));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.SALES_SIMPLE_EXAMPLE 
  (PROD NUMBER(38,0),   TOTAL_SALES NUMBER(10,2),   REGION VARCHAR(10));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.SALES_SIMPLE_EXAMPLE_UPDATED 
  (PROD NUMBER(38,0),   TOTAL_SALES NUMBER(10,2),   REGION VARCHAR(10));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.STATE_GOVERNORS 
 (STATE VARCHAR(128),  GOV_FIRST_NAME VARCHAR(20),  GOV_MIDDLE_NAME VARCHAR(20),  GOV_LAST_NAME VARCHAR(20),  PARTY VARCHAR(15),  DATE_TOOK_OFFICE DATE,  YEAR_TERM_ENDS NUMBER(11,0));

CREATE TABLE SQL_CLASS.WEBSITE 
  (CUSTOMER_NUMBER NUMBER(11,0),   WEB_PAGE VARCHAR(30),   CUSTOMER_TIMESTAMP TIMESTAMP_NTZ(6));

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.STATS_V AS
SELECT COL1, COL2, COL3, COL4, COL5, COL6
FROM SQL_CLASS.STATS_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.CUSTOMER_V (CUST_NO, CUST_NAME, PHONE) AS
SELECT CUSTOMER_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NAME, PHONE_NUMBER
FROM SQL_CLASS.CUSTOMER_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.ORDER_V (ORDER_NO, CUST_NO, ORDER_DATE, AMOUNT) AS
SELECT ORDER_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, ORDER_DATE, ORDER_TOTAL
FROM SQL_CLASS.ORDER_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.COURSE_V (COURSE_NO, COURSE_NAME, CREDITS, SEATS) AS
SELECT COURSE_ID, COURSE_NAME, CREDITS, SEATS
FROM SQL_CLASS.COURSE_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.STUDENT_V (STU_ID, LNAME, FNAME, CCODE, GPA) AS
SELECT STUDENT_ID, LAST_NAME, FIRST_NAME, CLASS_CODE, GRADE_PT
FROM SQL_CLASS.STUDENT_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.STUDENT_COURSE_V (STU_ID, CRSE_ID) AS
SELECT STUDENT_ID, COURSE_ID
FROM SQL_CLASS.STUDENT_COURSE_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.EMPLOYEE_V (EMP_NO, LNAME, FNAME, SAL, DEPT) AS
SELECT EMPLOYEE_NO, LAST_NAME, FIRST_NAME, SALARY, DEPT_NO
FROM SQL_CLASS.EMPLOYEE_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.DEPARTMENT_V (DEPT, DNAME, MGR, BUDGET) AS
SELECT DEPT_NO, DEPARTMENT_NAME, MGR_NO, BUDGET
FROM SQL_CLASS.DEPARTMENT_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.SALES_V (PRODUCT, DATE_OF_SALE, SALES_AMOUNT) AS
SELECT PRODUCT_ID, SALE_DATE, DAILY_SALES
FROM SQL_CLASS.SALES_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.JOB_V (JOBNO, JOBDESC) AS
SELECT JOB_NO, JOB_DESC
FROM SQL_CLASS.JOB_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.EMP_JOB_V (JOBNO, EMPNO) AS
SELECT JOB_NO, EMP_NO
FROM SQL_CLASS.EMP_JOB_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.NAMES_V AS
SELECT NAME
FROM SQL_CLASS.NAMES_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.SERVICES_V AS
SELECT SERVICE_CODE, SERVICE_DESC, SERVICE_PAY FROM SQL_CLASS.SERVICES;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.SUBSCRIBERS_V AS
SELECT SUBSCRIBER_NO, MEMBER_NO, LAST_NAME, FIRST_NAME, GENDER, SSN FROM SQL_CLASS.SUBSCRIBERS;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.HIERARCHY_V AS
SELECT EMPLOYEE_NO, DEPT_NO, FIRST_NAME, LAST_NAME, SALARY, POSITION_NAME, MGR_EMPLOYEE_NO FROM SQL_CLASS.HIERARCHY_TABLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.ADDRESSES_V AS
SELECT SUBSCRIBER_NO, STREET, CITY, STATE, ZIP, AREACODE, PHONE FROM SQL_CLASS.ADDRESSES;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.CLAIMS_V AS
SELECT CLAIM_ID ,CLAIM_DATE ,CLAIM_SERVICE ,SUBSCRIBER_NO ,MEMBER_NO ,CLAIM_AMT ,PROVIDER_NO FROM SQL_CLASS.CLAIMS;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.PROVIDERS_V AS
SELECT PROVIDER_CODE, PROVIDER_NAME,  P_ADDRESS, P_CITY, P_STATE, P_ZIP, P_ERROR_RATE FROM SQL_CLASS.PROVIDERS;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.BANK_SALES_V AS
SELECT PRODUCT_ID, PRODUCT_NAME, SALE_DATE, DAILY_SALES
FROM SQL_CLASS.BANK_SALES;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.EMPLOYEE_PHONE_V AS
SELECT FIRST_NAME, LAST_NAME, DEPT_NO, HOME_PHONE, WORK_PHONE, CELL_PHONE
FROM SQL_CLASS.EMPLOYEE_PHONE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.LAT_LONG_V AS
SELECT STATE, LATITUDE, LONGITUDE
FROM SQL_CLASS.LAT_LONG;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.PIVOT_TEST_REGION_ALL_V AS
SELECT REGION, SALES_PERSON, PRODUCT, QUANTITY, COST, SALE_DATE, DAILY_SALES
FROM SQL_CLASS.PIVOT_TEST_REGION_ALL;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.SALES_SIMPLE_EXAMPLE_V AS
SELECT PROD, TOTAL_SALES, REGION
FROM SQL_CLASS.SALES_SIMPLE_EXAMPLE;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.SALES_SIMPLE_EXAMPLE_UPDATED_V AS
SELECT PROD, TOTAL_SALES, REGION
FROM SQL_CLASS.SALES_SIMPLE_EXAMPLE_UPDATED;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.STATE_GOVERNORS_V AS
SELECT STATE, GOV_FIRST_NAME, GOV_MIDDLE_NAME, GOV_LAST_NAME, PARTY, DATE_TOOK_OFFICE, YEAR_TERM_ENDS
FROM SQL_CLASS.STATE_GOVERNORS;

CREATE VIEW SQL_VIEWS.WEBSITE_V AS
SELECT CUSTOMER_NUMBER, WEB_PAGE, CUSTOMER_TIMESTAMP
FROM SQL_CLASS.WEBSITE;
